        <article class="t-content__article-wrapper" data-article-content="">
                    <div class="t-content__section a-tag">
                            <span class="a-tag__wrapper">
                    AFRICA - HEALTH
                </span>
                    </div>
    
                        <h1 class="t-content__title a-page-title">WHO urges swift response as DRC hit by mutated mpox strain</h1>
    
            <p class="t-content__chapo">
                        The spread of mpox in Africa needs to be addressed urgently, the World Health Organization has warned, as more deaths were reported from a mutated strain of the virus in the Democratic Republic of Congo.&nbsp;        </p>
    
    
                        <div class="t-content__dates t-content__dates--reading-time">
                <p class="m-pub-dates"><span class="m-pub-dates__date">Issued on: <time datetime="2024-06-26T10:10:54+0000" pubdate="pubdate">26/06/2024 - 12:10</time></span></p>

    <div class="a-reading-time">
        <span class="a-svg a-svg--picto-clock" title="Reading time"></span> 1 min</div>
            </div>
            
    
                                                                            <div class="t-content__main-media">
                                                                                                                                                                                                                


<figure class="m-figure m-figure--16x9">            <picture>
            <source type="image/webp" srcset="https://s.rfi.fr/media/display/503a00a0-339c-11ef-a002-005056bfb2b6/w:246/p:16x9/000_32AV3BD.webp 246w,https://s.rfi.fr/media/display/503a00a0-339c-11ef-a002-005056bfb2b6/w:388/p:16x9/000_32AV3BD.webp 388w,https://s.rfi.fr/media/display/503a00a0-339c-11ef-a002-005056bfb2b6/w:720/p:16x9/000_32AV3BD.webp 720w,https://s.rfi.fr/media/display/503a00a0-339c-11ef-a002-005056bfb2b6/w:980/p:16x9/000_32AV3BD.webp 980w" sizes="(max-width: 1023px) 100vw, (min-width: 1024px) 980px">
    
    <img fetchpriority="high" src="https://s.rfi.fr/media/display/503a00a0-339c-11ef-a002-005056bfb2b6/w:980/p:16x9/000_32AV3BD.jpg" alt="A dangerous new strain of mpox is spreading quickly along the eastern border of the DRC, scientists have warned.&nbsp;" srcset="https://s.rfi.fr/media/display/503a00a0-339c-11ef-a002-005056bfb2b6/w:246/p:16x9/000_32AV3BD.jpg 246w,https://s.rfi.fr/media/display/503a00a0-339c-11ef-a002-005056bfb2b6/w:388/p:16x9/000_32AV3BD.jpg 388w,https://s.rfi.fr/media/display/503a00a0-339c-11ef-a002-005056bfb2b6/w:720/p:16x9/000_32AV3BD.jpg 720w,https://s.rfi.fr/media/display/503a00a0-339c-11ef-a002-005056bfb2b6/w:980/p:16x9/000_32AV3BD.jpg 980w" sizes="(max-width: 1023px) 100vw, (min-width: 1024px) 980px" width="980" height="551" loading="eager" class="m-figure__img lazy">
</picture>
                            <figcaption class="m-figure__caption">
                <span class="a-media-legend">A dangerous new strain of mpox is spreading quickly along the eastern border of the DRC, scientists have warned.&nbsp;</span>                <span class="a-media-legend">AFP - BRIAN W.J. MAHY</span>            </figcaption>
            </figure>
                                                                        </div>
                            
    
                    <div class="t-content__authors-tts">
                <div class="m-author-n-reading-time">
                    <div class="m-author-n-reading-time__authors">
                                        <div class="m-from-author">
                     <span class="m-from-author__by-label">
                By:
             </span>
                                                                <a href="/en/author/rfi/" title="RFI" class="m-from-author__name">
                        RFI
                    </a>
                
                                    <a class="a-twitter-follow-button" href="https://x.com/intent/follow?screen_name=RFI_En" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <span class="a-svg a-svg--picto-social-twitter-x-follow"></span>
    Follow
</a>
                
                                        </div>
                                                            </div>
                    </div>
        </div>
            
                                    <div class="t-content__body u-clearfix">
                                            <div class="m-interstitial">
    <div data-readmore-target="" class="m-interstitial__ad">
            <div class="m-block-ad " data-tms-ad-type="box" data-tms-ad-status="idle" data-tms-ad-pos="1">
        <div class="m-block-ad__label m-block-ad__label--report-enabled">
            <span class="m-block-ad__label__text">Advertising</span>
                            <button title="Report this ad" class="m-block-ad__label__report-link" rel="noopener" data-tms-ad-report="">
                                            <span class="a-svg a-svg--picto-report-ad"></span>
                                    </button>
                    </div>
        <div class="m-block-ad__content">
        </div>
    </div>
    </div>
        <button data-readmore-unlocker="" class="m-interstitial__unlock-btn">
        <span class="m-interstitial__unlock-btn__text">Read more
            <span class="a-svg a-svg--picto-chevron-bottom-small"></span>
        </span>
    </button>
    </div>
                                                                <p>Mpox, formerly known as <a href="https://www.who.int/news-room/fact-sheets/detail/monkeypox" target="_blank">monkeypox</a>, from the same family as smallpox, causes flu-like symptoms and pus-filled lesions. Most cases are mild but it can also be deadly.&nbsp;</p><p>"There is a critical need to address the recent surge in mpox cases in Africa," Rosamund Lewis, the WHO's technical lead for mpox, told journalists on Tuesday.&nbsp;</p><p>A dangerous new strain of mpox was spreading quickly along the eastern border of the DRC and was "incredibly worrying", scientists warned separately.&nbsp;</p><p>A mutated version of the <a href="https://www.cdc.gov/poxvirus/mpox/about/index.html#:~:text=Clade I is endemic to,than 99.9% of people survive." target="_blank">clade I</a> mpox endemic in Congo for decades&nbsp;had fatality rates of around 5 percent in adults and 10 percent in children said biomedical engineer John Claude Udahemuka, who has been working on an outbreak in the hard-to-reach South Kivu province.&nbsp;</p><ul>  	<li><strong><a href="https://www.rfi.fr/en/international/20240620-world-leaders-announce-1-2bn-to-create-african-vaccine-market" target="_self">World leaders announce $1.2bn to create 'African vaccine market'</a></strong></li></ul><h2>Hundreds dead</h2><p>This year, roughly 8,600 mpox cases have been reported in the <a href="https://www.rfi.fr/en/tag/drc/" target="_self" class="gtm-add-suggested-tag">DRC</a> with 410 deaths, Cris Kacita, the doctor in charge of operations in the country's mpox control programme, told Reuters last week.&nbsp;</p><p>"At the rate things are going, we risk becoming a source of cases for other countries," said Kacita. South Kivu borders <a href="https://www.rfi.fr/en/tag/rwanda/" target="_self" class="gtm-add-suggested-tag">Rwanda</a> and <a href="https://www.rfi.fr/en/tag/burundi/" target="_self" class="gtm-add-suggested-tag">Burundi</a>.&nbsp;</p><p>In South Kivu, researchers said the new strain was spreading partly by sexual contact among men and women, and particularly among sex workers. &nbsp;</p><p>It is also being spread by non-sexual contact in places including schools.&nbsp;</p><p>In 2022 the WHO declared a public health emergency after an outbreak in <a href="https://www.rfi.fr/en/tag/europe/" target="_self" class="gtm-add-suggested-tag">Europe</a> and the US that centred on the gay community.&nbsp;</p><p>It was brought under control by vaccinating vulnerable groups, but the vaccines were not&nbsp;available&nbsp;in the DRC.&nbsp;</p><p><em>(with newswires)</em></p>
